The key components include:\\n\\n1. **Listener Interfaces**: StreamsRebalanceListener (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/StreamsRebalanceListener.java) is an interface for handling streams group rebalance events, with methods onTasksRevoked, onTasksAssigned, and onAllTasksLost.\\n\\n2. **Callback Handling**: ConsumerRebalanceListenerInvoker (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/ConsumerRebalanceListenerInvoker.java) encapsulates the invocation of ConsumerRebalanceListener callback methods (onPartitionsAssigned, onPartitionsRevoked, onPartitionsLost). StreamsRebalanceListenerInvoker (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/StreamsRebalanceListenerInvoker.java) similarly wraps callback invocations for the streams rebalance listener.\\n\\n3. **Method Name Enumeration**: ConsumerRebalanceListenerMethodName (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/ConsumerRebalanceListenerMethodName.java) is an enum providing static names for the ConsumerRebalanceListener methods.\\n\\n4. **Rebalance Data Structures**: StreamsRebalanceData (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/StreamsRebalanceData.java) holds the data required for participating in the Streams rebalance protocol, including TaskId, HostInfo, EndpointPartitions, Assignment, Subtopology, and TopicInfo inner classes.\\n\\n5. **Event-Driven Architecture**: ConsumerRebalanceListenerCallbackNeededEvent (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/events/ConsumerRebalanceListenerCallbackNeededEvent.java) signals when the network I/O thread requests invocation of a callback method. ConsumerRebalanceListenerCallbackCompletedEvent (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/events/ConsumerRebalanceListenerCallbackCompletedEvent.java) signals that the application thread has executed a callback.\\n\\n6. **Metrics Management**: RebalanceMetricsManager (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/metrics/RebalanceMetricsManager.java) is an abstract base class for rebalance metrics. ConsumerRebalanceMetricsManager (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/metrics/ConsumerRebalanceMetricsManager.java) extends it to track consumer rebalance latency, frequency, and failures. ShareRebalanceMetricsManager (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/metrics/ShareRebalanceMetricsManager.java) extends RebalanceMetricsManager for share group rebalances.
